--- Commit Message ---
LU-17525 llite: unaligned DIO interop page alignment

Correctly size brw/ptlrpc bulk ops I/O between archs with differing
page sizes (ex: 64k client and 4k server).

Since the number of MDs need for a bulk are not stable until all the
pages are added we have two parts to interop calculation.

In the fist step if this is an unaligned dio bulk with a 64k offset
greater than 4k in size calculate the initial MD utilization
as if first partial page is 64k in length.

In the second step after bulk is sized and split across 1 or more
MDs, if the number of MDs:
 - if the number of MDs is 1, clear the interop flag
 - if the number of MDs is 3 or more, keep the interop flag
 - if the number of MDs is 2 and the size with the 64k offset does
   not exceed the LNET_MUT then collapse the extra MD.
This is done by assuming the first page is 64k length.

Additionally fixup OBD_CONNECT2_UNALIGNED_DIO and add a ZFS osd
heuristic check. No unaligned DIO should be performed with older
zfs-osd, however unaligned dio with unpatched ldiskfs servers is
allowed for most cases. Allow I/O that will trigger the page
size interop issue will get fail with -EINVAL, were previously
these i/o would fail sending with an error:

LNetError: 7386:0:(lib-ptl.c:189:lnet_try_match_md()) Matching packet
   from 12345-10.240.22.81@tcp, match 1789613636069888 length 1044481
   too big: 983041 left, 983041 allowed

triggering the MD to be resent, however the size calcuations reamin
unchanged resulting in a hang.

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2024-03-06 01:23:58.000000000) ---
Patch Set 10: Code-Review-1

(13 comments)

Shaun, thanks for looking into this issue.  It is hard to understand the full details/impact of the issue with only the description in LU-17525 to go on, so I've commented based on my best understanding of what the issue is, but it may still need some refinement.

In any case, I don't think the approach taken here works properly if a 64KB-page client is writing to an old server that doesn't understand the bit in ioo_max_brw.  In that case, the server will just blindly continue to do the wrong thing with these writes.

I think a reasonable solution would be to use a connect-time flag that indicates the OST/MDT has support for these "unaligned UDIO" read/write bulk operations, and only if that feature is supported or the client has 4KB PAGE_SIZE, then the client can use UDIO.  That puts the burden of compatibility on the client (which knows its PAGE_SIZE and controls UDIO) and not on the old server, which may have no idea that UDIO even exists.

There is already OBD_CONNECT2_UNALIGNED_DIO that has been added in patch https://review.whamcloud.com/51126 "LU-13805 llite: Implement unaligned DIO connect flag".  That was landed as commit v2_15_59-6-g0e6e60b123, so it has been around a while, but should not yet be used by any release so could potentially grow in scope to cover this 64KB PAGE_SIZE alignment issue as well.

This would mean *not* setting OBD_CONNECT2_UNALIGNED_DIO on clients that have PAGE_SIZE > 4096 (causing them to not use UDIO with unpatched servers), and fixing LU-17597 to actually make that interop check work properly.  The server-side changes to handle the obd_ioobj flag would also fall under that connect flag.

Ah, I think I understand, yes we can add a UDIO_64K_BULK flag.

> I understand, yes we can add a UDIO_64K_BULK flag

I was thinking about a separate flag also, but since the UNALIGNED_DIO flag has only been landed in 2.15.58 I don't think we *need* a new flag, and can instead change the meaning of the existing UNALIGNED_DIO flag, unless there is a reason not to do so.
